e.g., \"us\", \"eu\"\nPROCESSOR_ID = \"your-processor-id\"  # Document AI processor ID\n\n# Fields to extract from invoice\nFIELDS_TO_EXTRACT = [\n    \"Invoice Number\",\n    \"Invoice Date\",\n    \"Supplier Name\",\n    \"Supplier Address\",\n    \"Total Amount\",\n    \"Due Date\",\n    \"Line Items\",  # This can be a list of dicts\n]\n\n# ------------------------------\n# DOCUMENT AI CLIENT SETUP\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef get_documentai_client():\n    \"\"\"\n    Returns a Document AI client.\n    \"\"\"\n    client = documentai.DocumentUnderstandingServiceClient(\n        client_options=ClientOptions(api_endpoint=f\"{LOCATION}-documentai.googleapis.com\")\n    )\n    return client\n\ndef get_processor_client():\n    \"\"\"\n    Returns a Document AI Processors client.\n    \"\"\"\n    client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient(\n        client_options=ClientOptions(api_endpoint=f\"{LOCATION}-documentai.googleapis.com\")\n    )\n    return client\n\n# ------------------------------\n# DOCUMENT PROCESSING\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef process_document(file_path: str) -> documentai.Document:\n    \"\"\"\n    Sends a document (PDF or image) to Google Document AI and returns the parsed Document object.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Read the file into memory\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as f:\n        file_content = f.read()\n\n    mime_type = \"application/pdf\" if file_path.lower().endswith(\".pdf\") else \"image/jpeg\"\n\n    # Instantiates a client\n    client = get_processor_client()\n\n    # The full resource name of the processor\n    name = f\"projects/{PROJECT_ID}/locations/{LOCATION}/processors/{PROCESSOR_ID}\"\n\n    # Prepare the raw document\n    raw_document = documentai.RawDocument(content=file_content, mime_type=mime_type)\n\n    # Prepare the request\n    request = documentai.ProcessRequest(\n        name=name,\n        raw_document=raw_document,\n    )\n\n    # Process the document\n    result = client.process_document(request=request)\n    document = result.document\n    return document\n\n# ------------------------------\n# FIELD EXTRACTION\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef extract_fields(document: documentai.Document) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Extracts specified fields from the Document AI response.\n    \"\"\"\n    extracted = {}\n\n    # Helper to get text from a documentai.Document.TextAnchor\n    def get_text(text_anchor: documentai.Document.TextAnchor) -> str:\n        response_text = \"\"\n        for segment in text_anchor.text_segments:\n            start_index = segment.start_index\n            end_index = segment.end_index\n            response_text += document.text[start_index:end_index]\n        return response_text.strip()\n\n    # Document AI Invoice processor outputs entities\n    for entity in document.entities:\n        entity_type = entity.type_\n        entity_text = get_text(entity.text_anchor)\n        if entity_type == \"invoice_id\" and \"Invoice Number\" in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            extracted[\"Invoice Number\"] = entity_text\n        elif entity_type == \"invoice_date\" and \"Invoice Date\" in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            extracted[\"Invoice Date\"] = entity_text\n        elif entity_type == \"supplier_name\" and \"Supplier Name\" in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            extracted[\"Supplier Name\"] = entity_text\n        elif entity_type == \"supplier_address\" and \"Supplier Address\" in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            extracted[\"Supplier Address\"] = entity_text\n        elif entity_type == \"total_amount\" and \"Total Amount\" in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            extracted[\"Total Amount\"] = entity_text\n        elif entity_type == \"due_date\" and \"Due Date\" in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            extracted[\"Due Date\"] = entity_text\n        elif entity_type == \"line_item\" and \"Line Items\" in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            # Line items can be multiple\n            if \"Line Items\" not in extracted:\n                extracted[\"Line Items\"] = []\n            # Extract details from sub-entities\n            line_item = {}\n            for prop in entity.properties:\n                prop_type = prop.type_\n                prop_text = get_text(prop.text_anchor)\n                line_item[prop_type] = prop_text\n            extracted[\"Line Items\"].append(line_item)\n\n    # Optionally, add fallback for missing fields\n    for field in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n        if field not in extracted:\n            extracted[field] = None\n\n    return extracted\n\n# ------------------------------\n# OUTPUT FORMATTING\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef save_as_json(data: Dict[str, Any], output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Saves the extracted data as a JSON file.\n    \"\"\"\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        json.dump(data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\ndef save_as_csv(data: Dict[str, Any], output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Saves the extracted data as a CSV file.\n    Handles line items as a nested CSV.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Flatten top-level fields\n    fieldnames = [field for field in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT if field != \"Line Items\"]\n    # Write main invoice data\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", newline='', encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        row = {field: data.get(field, \"\") for field in fieldnames}\n        writer.writerow(row)\n\n        # Write line items if present\n        if data.get(\"Line Items\"):\n            # Assume all line items have the same keys\n            line_item_keys = set()\n            for item in data[\"Line Items\"]:\n                line_item_keys.update(item.keys())\n            line_item_keys = list(line_item_keys)\n            csvfile.write(\"\\nLine Items:\\n\")\n            line_item_writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=line_item_keys)\n            line_item_writer.writeheader()\n            for item in data[\"Line Items\"]:\n                line_item_writer.writerow(item)\n\n# ------------------------------\n# MAIN SCRIPT\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"Extract specified fields from supplier invoices using Google Document AI.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"input_file\",\n        help=\"Path to the invoice file (PDF or image) to process.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--output\",\n        help=\"Path to the output file (JSON or CSV).\",\n        required=True\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--format\",\n        choices=[\"json\", \"csv\"],\n        default=\"json\",\n        help=\"Output format: json or csv (default: json).\"\n    )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    # Check Google Application Credentials\n    if not os.getenv(\"GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS\"):\n        print(\"ERROR: Set the GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS environment variable to your service account JSON file.\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Process document\n    print(f\"Processing document: {args.input_file}\")\n    try:\n        document = process_document(args.input_file)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"ERROR: Document processing failed: {e}\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(2)\n\n    # Extract fields\n    extracted_data = extract_fields(document)\n    print(f\"Extracted fields: {json.dumps(extracted_data, indent=2)}\")\n\n    # Save output\n    if args.format == \"json\":\n        save_as_json(extracted_data, args.output)\n        print(f\"Results saved to {args.output} (JSON)\")\n    else:\n        save_as_csv(extracted_data, args.output)\n        print(f\"Results saved to {args.output} (CSV)\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()",

                        "import os\nimport sys\nimport argparse\nimport json\nimport csv\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\n\nfrom google.cloud import documentai_v1 as documentai\nfrom google.api_core.client_options import ClientOptions\n\n# ------------------------------\n# CONFIGURATION\n# ------------------------------\n\n# Set your Google Cloud project details here\nPROJECT_ID = \"your-gcp-project-id\"  # <-- UPDATE THIS\nLOCATION = \"us\"  # e.g., \"us\", \"eu\"\nPROCESSOR_ID = \"your-processor-id\"  # <-- UPDATE THIS\n\n# Fields to extract from invoice\nFIELDS_TO_EXTRACT = [\n    \"Invoice Number\",\n    \"Invoice Date\",\n    \"Supplier Name\",\n    \"Supplier Address\",\n    \"Total Amount\",\n    \"Due Date\",\n    \"Line Items\",  # This can be a list of dicts\n]\n\n# ------------------------------\n# DOCUMENT AI CLIENT SETUP\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef get_processor_client() -> documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient:\n    \"\"\"\n    Returns a Document AI Processors client.\n    \"\"\"\n    client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient(\n        client_options=ClientOptions(api_endpoint=f\"{LOCATION}-documentai.googleapis.com\")\n    )\n    return client\n\n# ------------------------------\n# DOCUMENT PROCESSING\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef process_document(file_path: str) -> documentai.Document:\n    \"\"\"\n    Sends a document (PDF or image) to Google Document AI and returns the parsed Document object.\n    Handles both PDF and common image formats.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Read file into memory\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as f:\n        file_content = f.read()\n\n    # Determine MIME type\n    ext = os.path.splitext(file_path)[1].lower()\n    if ext == \".pdf\":\n        mime_type = \"application/pdf\"\n    elif ext in [\".jpg\", \".jpeg\"]:\n        mime_type = \"image/jpeg\"\n    elif ext == \".png\":\n        mime_type = \"image/png\"\n    elif ext == \".tiff\" or ext == \".tif\":\n        mime_type = \"image/tiff\"\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(f\"Unsupported file extension: {ext}\")\n\n    client = get_processor_client()\n    name = f\"projects/{PROJECT_ID}/locations/{LOCATION}/processors/{PROCESSOR_ID}\"\n\n    raw_document = documentai.RawDocument(content=file_content, mime_type=mime_type)\n    request = documentai.ProcessRequest(name=name, raw_document=raw_document)\n\n    # Prepare for line items\n    extracted[\"Line Items\"] = []\n\n    for entity in document.entities:\n        entity_type = entity.type_\n        field_name = ENTITY_TYPE_TO_FIELD.get(entity_type)\n        entity_text = get_text(entity.text_anchor)\n        if field_name is None:\n            continue\n\n        if field_name == \"Line Items\":\n            # Use prop.type_ as key, but you can map to friendlier names if needed\n                line_item[prop_type] = prop_text\n            # Add confidence if needed: line_item['confidence'] = entity.confidence\n            extracted[\"Line Items\"].append(line_item)\n        else:\n            # Only set if not already set (first occurrence)\n            if field_name not in extracted or not extracted[field_name]:\n                extracted[field_name] = entity_text\n\n    # Remove \"Line Items\" if none found\n    if not extracted[\"Line Items\"]:\n        extracted.pop(\"Line Items\")\n\n    # Ensure all fields are present in output\n    for field in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n        if field not in extracted:\n            extracted[field] = None\n\n    return extracted\n\n# ------------------------------\n# OUTPUT FORMATTING\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef save_as_json(data: Dict[str, Any], output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Saves the extracted data as a JSON file.\n    \"\"\"\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        json.dump(data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\ndef save_as_csv(data: Dict[str, Any], output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Saves the extracted data as a CSV file.\n    Handles line items as a nested CSV.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Top-level fields (excluding line items)\n    fieldnames = [f for f in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT if f != \"Line Items\"]\n\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", newline='', encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        row = {field: data.get(field, \"\") for field in fieldnames}\n        writer.writerow(row)\n\n        # Write line items if present\n        if data.get(\"Line Items\"):\n            csvfile.write(\"\\nLine Items:\\n\")\n            line_items = data[\"Line Items\"]\n            # Gather all possible keys for line items\n            all_keys = set()\n            for item in line_items:\n                all_keys.update(item.keys())\n            all_keys = list(all_keys)\n            line_writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=all_keys)\n            line_writer.writeheader()\n            for item in line_items:\n                line_writer.writerow(item)\n\n# ------------------------------\n# MAIN SCRIPT\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"Extract specified fields from supplier invoices using Google Document AI.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"input_file\",\n        help=\"Path to the invoice file (PDF or image) to process.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--output\",\n        help=\"Path to the output file (JSON or CSV).\",\n        required=True\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--format\",\n        choices=[\"json\", \"csv\"],\n        default=\"json\",\n        help=\"Output format: json or csv (default: json).\"\n    )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    #                         "import os\nimport sys\nimport argparse\nimport json\nimport csv\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional\n\nfrom google.cloud import documentai_v1 as documentai\nfrom google.api_core.client_options import ClientOptions\n\n# ------------------------------\n# CONFIGURATION\n# ------------------------------\n\n# Set your Google Cloud project details here\nPROJECT_ID = \"your-gcp-project-id\"        # <-- Change this\nLOCATION = \"us\"                           # e.g., \"us\", \"eu\"\nPROCESSOR_ID = \"your-processor-id\"        # <-- Change this\n\n# Fields to extract from invoice\nFIELDS_TO_EXTRACT = [\n    \"Invoice Number\",\n    \"Invoice Date\",\n    \"Supplier Name\",\n    \"Supplier Address\",\n    \"Total Amount\",\n    \"Due Date\",\n    \"Line Items\",  # This can be a list of dicts\n]\n\n# ------------------------------\n# DOCUMENT AI CLIENT SETUP\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef get_processor_client() -> documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient:\n    \"\"\"\n    Returns a Document AI Processors client.\n    \"\"\"\n    client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient(\n        client_options=ClientOptions(api_endpoint=f\"{LOCATION}-documentai.googleapis.com\")\n    )\n    return client\n\n# ------------------------------\n# DOCUMENT PROCESSING\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef process_document(file_path: str) -> documentai.Document:\n    \"\"\"\n    Sends a document (PDF or image) to Google Document AI and returns the parsed Document object.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Read the file into memory\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as f:\n        file_content = f.read()\n\n    # Determine MIME type\n    ext = os.path.splitext(file_path)[1].lower()\n    if ext == \".pdf\":\n        mime_type = \"application/pdf\"\n    elif ext in [\".jpg\", \".jpeg\"]:\n        mime_type = \"image/jpeg\"\n    elif ext == \".png\":\n        mime_type = \"image/png\"\n    elif ext == \".tiff\" or ext == \".tif\":\n        mime_type = \"image/tiff\"\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(f\"Unsupported file extension: {ext}\")\n\n    client = get_processor_client()\n    name = f\"projects/{PROJECT_ID}/locations/{LOCATION}/processors/{PROCESSOR_ID}\"\n\n    raw_document = documentai.RawDocument(content=file_content, mime_type=mime_type)\n    request = documentai.ProcessRequest(\n        name=name,\n        raw_document=raw_document,\n    )\n\n    result = client.process_document(request=request)\n    document = result.document\n    return document\n\n# ------------------------------\n# FIELD EXTRACTION\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef extract_fields(document: documentai.Document) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Extracts specified fields from the Document AI response.\n    \"\"\"\n    extracted = {}\n\n    # Helper to get text from a documentai.Document.TextAnchor\n    def get_text(text_anchor: documentai.Document.TextAnchor) -> str:\n        response_text = \"\"\n        for segment in text_anchor.text_segments:\n            start_index = segment.start_index\n            end_index = segment.end_index\n            response_text += document.text[start_index:end_index]\n        return response_text.strip()\n\n    # Map Document AI entity types to our field names\n    entity_map = {\n        \"invoice_id\": \"Invoice Number\",\n        \"invoice_date\": \"Invoice Date\",\n        \"supplier_name\": \"Supplier Name\",\n        \"supplier_address\": \"Supplier Address\",\n        \"total_amount\": \"Total Amount\",\n        \"due_date\": \"Due Date\",\n        \"line_item\": \"Line Items\"\n    }\n\n    for entity in document.entities:\n        entity_type = entity.type_\n        field_name = entity_map.get(entity_type)\n        if not field_name or field_name not in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            continue\n\n        entity_text = get_text(entity.text_anchor)\n\n        if entity_type == \"line_item\":\n            # Line items can be multiple\n            if \"Line Items\" not in extracted:\n                extracted[\"Line Items\"] = []\n            line_item = {}\n            for prop in entity.properties:\n                prop_type = prop.type_\n                prop_text = get_text(prop.text_anchor)\n                # Use prop_type as key, but you may want to map it to a friendlier name\n                line_item[prop_type] = prop_text\n            extracted[\"Line Items\"].append(line_item)\n        else:\n            extracted[field_name] = entity_text\n\n    # Ensure all fields are present\n    for field in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n        if field not in extracted:\n            extracted[field] = None\n\n    return extracted\n\n# ------------------------------\n# OUTPUT FORMATTING\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef save_as_json(data: Dict[str, Any], output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Saves the extracted data as a JSON file.\n    \"\"\"\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        json.dump(data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\ndef save_as_csv(data: Dict[str, Any], output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Saves the extracted data as a CSV file.\n    Handles line items as a nested CSV.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Flatten top-level fields except line items\n    fieldnames = [field for field in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT if field != \"Line Items\"]\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", newline='', encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fieldnames)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        row = {field: data.get(field, \"\") for field in fieldnames}\n        writer.writerow(row)\n\n        # Write line items if present\n        if data.get(\"Line Items\"):\n            line_items = data[\"Line Items\"]\n            if line_items:\n                # Write a blank row as separator\n                csvfile.write(\"\\n\")\n                # Write line item headers\n                line_item_keys = set()\n                for item in line_items:\n                    line_item_keys.update(item.keys())\n                line_item_keys = list(line_item_keys)\n                line_item_writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=line_item_keys)\n                csvfile.write(\"Line Items:\\n\")\n                line_item_writer.writeheader()\n                for item in line_items:\n                    line_item_writer.writerow(item)\n\n# ------------------------------\n# MAIN SCRIPT\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"Extract specified fields from supplier invoices using Google Document AI.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"input_file\",\n        help=\"Path to the invoice file (PDF or image) to process.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--output\",\n        help=\"Path to the output file (JSON or CSV).\",\n        required=True\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--format\",\n        choices=[\"json\", \"csv\"],\n        default=\"json\",\n        help=\"Output format: json or csv (default: json).\"\n    )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    # Check Google Application Credentials\n    if not os.getenv(\"GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS\"):\n        print(\"ERROR: Set the GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS environment variable to your service account JSON file.\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Process document\n    print(f\"Processing document: {args.input_file}\")\n    try:\n        document = process_document(args.input_file)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"ERROR: Document processing failed: {e}\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(2)\n\n    # Extract fields\n    extracted_data = extract_fields(document)\n    print(f\"Extracted fields:\\n{json.dumps(extracted_data, indent=2)}\")\n\n    # Save output\n    if args.format == \"json\":\n        save_as_json(extracted_data, args.output)\n        print(f\"Results saved to {args.output} (JSON)\")\n    else:\n        save_as_csv(extracted_data, args.output)\n        print(f\"Results saved to {args.output} (CSV)\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

Read the file into memory\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as f:\n        file_content = f.read()\n\n    # Determine MIME type\n    ext = os.path.splitext(file_path)[1].lower()\n    if ext == \".pdf\":\n        mime_type = \"application/pdf\"\n    elif ext in [\".jpg\", \".jpeg\"]:\n        mime_type = \"image/jpeg\"\n    elif ext == \".png\":\n        mime_type = \"image/png\"\n    elif ext == \".tif\" or ext == \".tiff\":\n        mime_type = \"image/tiff\"\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(f\"Unsupported file type: {ext}\")\n\n    client = get_processor_client()\n    name = f\"projects/{PROJECT_ID}/locations/{LOCATION}/processors/{PROCESSOR_ID}\"\n\n    raw_document = documentai.RawDocument(content=file_content, mime_type=mime_type)\n    request = documentai.ProcessRequest(name=name, raw_document=raw_document)\n    result = client.process_document(request=request)\n    document = result.document\n    return document\n\n# ------------------------------\n# FIELD EXTRACTION\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef extract_fields(document: documentai.Document) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Extracts specified fields from the Document AI response.\n    Handles missing fields gracefully.\n    \"\"\"\n    extracted = {}\n\n    def get_text(text_anchor: documentai.Document.TextAnchor) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Helper to get text from a documentai.Document.TextAnchor.\n        \"\"\"\n        response_text = \"\"\n        for segment in text_anchor.text_segments:\n            start_index = segment.start_index\n            end_index = segment.end_index\n            response_text += document.text[start_index:end_index]\n        return response_text.strip()\n\n    # Map Document AI entity types to our field names\n    entity_type_map = {\n        \"invoice_id\": \"Invoice Number\",\n        \"invoice_date\": \"Invoice Date\",\n        \"supplier_name\": \"Supplier Name\",\n        \"supplier_address\": \"Supplier Address\",\n        \"total_amount\": \"Total Amount\",\n        \"due_date\": \"Due Date\",\n        \"line_item\": \"Line Items\",\n    }\n\n    for entity in document.entities:\n        entity_type = entity.type_\n        field_name = entity_type_map.get(entity_type)\n        if not field_name or field_name not in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            continue\n\n        entity_text = get_text(entity.text_anchor)\n\n        if field_name == \"Line Items\":\n            # Write main invoice data\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", newline='', encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=main_fields)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        writer.writerow(main_row)\n\n        # Write line items if present\n        line_items = data.get(\"Line Items\") or []\n        if line_items:\n            # Write a blank line and a header for line items\n            csvfile.write(\"\\n\")\n            csvfile.write(\"Line Items:\\n\")\n            # Collect all possible keys in line items\n            all_keys = set()\n            for item in line_items:\n                all_keys.update(item.keys())\n            all_keys = list(all_keys)\n            line_item_writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=all_keys)\n            line_item_writer.writeheader()\n            for item in line_items:\n                line_item_writer.writerow(item)\n\n# ------------------------------\n# MAIN SCRIPT\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"Extract specified fields from supplier invoices using Google Document AI.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"input_file\",\n        help=\"Path to the invoice file (PDF or image) to process.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--output\",\n        help=\"Path to the output file (JSON or CSV).\",\n        required=True\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--format\",\n        choices=[\"json\", \"csv\"],\n        default=\"json\",\n        help=\"Output format: json or csv (default: json).\"\n    )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    # Collect all possible keys in line items\n            all_keys = set()\n            for item in line_items:\n                all_keys.update(item.keys())\n            all_keys = list(all_keys)\n            line_item_writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=all_keys)\n            line_item_writer.writeheader()\n            for item in line_items:\n                line_item_writer.writerow(item)\n\n# ------------------------------\n# MAIN SCRIPT\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"Extract specified fields from supplier invoices using Google Document AI.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"input_file\",\n        help=\"Path to the invoice file (PDF or image) to process.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--output\",\n        help=\"Path to the output file (JSON or CSV).\",\n        required=True\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--format\",\n        choices=[\"json\", \"csv\"],\n        default=\"json\",\n        help=\"Output format: json or csv (default: json).\"\n    )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    # This can be a list of dicts\n]\n\n# ------------------------------\n# DOCUMENT AI CLIENT SETUP\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef get_processor_client():\n    \"\"\"\n    Returns a Document AI Processors client.\n    \"\"\"\n    client = documentai.DocumentProcessorServiceClient(\n        client_options=ClientOptions(api_endpoint=f\"{LOCATION}-documentai.googleapis.com\")\n    )\n    return client\n\n# ------------------------------\n# DOCUMENT PROCESSING\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef process_document(file_path: str) -> documentai.Document:\n    \"\"\"\n    Sends a document (PDF or image) to Google Document AI and returns the parsed Document object.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Read the file into memory\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as f:\n        file_content = f.read()\n\n    # Determine MIME type\n    ext = os.path.splitext(file_path)[1].lower()\n    if ext == \".pdf\":\n        mime_type = \"application/pdf\"\n    elif ext in [\".jpg\", \".jpeg\"]:\n        mime_type = \"image/jpeg\"\n    elif ext == \".png\":\n        mime_type = \"image/png\"\n    elif ext in [\".tif\", \".tiff\"]:\n        mime_type = \"image/tiff\"\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(f\"Unsupported file type: {ext}\")\n\n    client = get_processor_client()\n    name = f\"projects/{PROJECT_ID}/locations/{LOCATION}/processors/{PROCESSOR_ID}\"\n\n    raw_document = documentai.RawDocument(content=file_content, mime_type=mime_type)\n    request = documentai.ProcessRequest(name=name, raw_document=raw_document)\n    result = client.process_document(request=request)\n    document = result.document\n    return document\n\n# ------------------------------\n# FIELD EXTRACTION\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef extract_fields(document: documentai.Document) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Extracts specified fields from the Document AI response.\n    Handles missing fields gracefully.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    extracted = {}\n\n    def get_text(text_anchor: documentai.Document.TextAnchor) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Helper to get text from a documentai.Document.TextAnchor.\n        \"\"\"\n        response_text = \"\"\n        for segment in text_anchor.text_segments:\n            start_index = segment.start_index\n            end_index = segment.end_index\n            response_text += document.text[start_index:end_index]\n        return response_text.strip()\n\n    # Map Document AI entity types to our field names\n    entity_type_map = {\n        \"invoice_id\": \"Invoice Number\",\n        \"invoice_date\": \"Invoice Date\",\n        \"supplier_name\": \"Supplier Name\",\n        \"supplier_address\": \"Supplier Address\",\n        \"total_amount\": \"Total Amount\",\n        \"due_date\": \"Due Date\",\n        \"line_item\": \"Line Items\",\n    }\n\n    for entity in document.entities:\n        entity_type = entity.type_\n        field_name = entity_type_map.get(entity_type)\n        if not field_name or field_name not in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            continue\n\n        entity_text = get_text(entity.text_anchor)\n\n        if field_name == \"Line Items\":\n            # Line items can be multiple\n            if \"Line Items\" not in extracted:\n                extracted[\"Line Items\"] = []\n            line_item = {}\n            for prop in entity.properties:\n                prop_type = prop.type_\n                prop_text = get_text(prop.text_anchor)\n                line_item[prop_type] = prop_text\n            extracted[\"Line Items\"].append(line_item)\n        else:\n            # For non-list fields, only set if not already set (take first occurrence)\n            if field_name not in extracted:\n                extracted[field_name] = entity_text\n\n    # Ensure all fields are present\n    for field in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n        if field not in extracted:\n            extracted[field] = None if field != \"Line Items\" else []\n\n    return extracted\n\n# ------------------------------\n# OUTPUT FORMATTING\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef save_as_json(data: Dict[str, Any], output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Saves the extracted data as a JSON file.\n    \"\"\"\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        json.dump(data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\ndef save_as_csv(data: Dict[str, Any], output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Saves the extracted data as a CSV file.\n    Handles line items as a nested CSV (writes two CSVs: main and line items).\n    \"\"\"\n    # Main invoice fields (excluding line items)\n    main_fields = [field for field in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT if field != \"Line Items\"]\n    main_row = {field: data.get(field, \"\") for field in main_fields}\n\n    # Write main invoice data\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", newline='', encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=main_fields)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        writer.writerow(main_row)\n\n        # Write line items if present\n        line_items = data.get(\"Line Items\") or []\n        if line_items:\n            # Write a blank line and a header for line items\n            csvfile.write(\"\\n\")\n            csvfile.write(\"Line Items:\\n\")\n            # Collect all possible keys in line items\n            all_keys = set()\n            for item in line_items:\n                all_keys.update(item.keys())\n            all_keys = list(all_keys)\n            line_item_writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=all_keys)\n            line_item_writer.writeheader()\n            for item in line_items:\n                line_item_writer.writerow(item)\n\n# ------------------------------\n# MAIN SCRIPT\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"Extract specified fields from supplier invoices using Google Document AI.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"input_file\",\n        help=\"Path to the invoice file (PDF or image) to process.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--output\",\n        help=\"Path to the output file (JSON or CSV).\",\n        required=True\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--format\",\n        choices=[\"json\", \"csv\"],\n        default=\"json\",\n        help=\"Output format: json or csv (default: json).\"\n    )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    # Check Google Application Credentials\n    if not os.getenv(\"GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS\"):\n        print(\"ERROR: Set the GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS environment variable to your service account JSON file.\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Process document\n    print(f\"Processing document: {args.input_file}\")\n    try:\n        document = process_document(args.input_file)\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"ERROR: Document processing failed: {e}\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(2)\n\n    # Extract fields\n    extracted_data = extract_fields(document)\n    print(f\"Extracted fields:\\n{json.dumps(extracted_data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)}\")\n\n    # Save output\n    if args.format == \"json\":\n        save_as_json(extracted_data, args.output)\n        print(f\"Results saved to {args.output} (JSON)\")\n    else:\n        save_as_csv(extracted_data, args.output)\n        print(f\"Results saved to {args.output} (CSV)\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

Items\",\n]\n\ndef extract_fields(document) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    def get_text(text_anchor):\n        response_text = \"\"\n        if not text_anchor.text_segments:\n            return \"\"\n        for segment in text_anchor.text_segments:\n            start_index = segment.start_index\n            end_index = segment.end_index\n            response_text += document.text[start_index:end_index]\n        return response_text.strip()\n\n    entity_type_map = {\n        \"invoice_id\": \"Invoice Number\",\n        \"invoice_date\": \"Invoice Date\",\n        \"supplier_name\": \"Supplier Name\",\n        \"supplier_address\": \"Supplier Address\",\n        \"total_amount\": \"Total Amount\",\n        \"due_date\": \"Due Date\",\n        \"line_item\": \"Line Items\",\n    }\n\n    extracted = {}\n\n    for entity in document.entities:\n        entity_type = entity.type_\n        field_name = entity_type_map.get(entity_type)\n        if not field_name or field_name not in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n            continue\n\n        entity_text = get_text(entity.text_anchor)\n\n        if field_name == \"Line Items\":\n            if \"Line Items\" not in extracted:\n                extracted[\"Line Items\"] = []\n            line_item = {}\n            for prop in entity.properties:\n                prop_type = prop.type_\n                prop_text = get_text(prop.text_anchor)\n                line_item[prop_type] = prop_text\n            extracted[\"Line Items\"].append(line_item)\n        else:\n            if field_name not in extracted:\n                extracted[field_name] = entity_text\n\n    for field in FIELDS_TO_EXTRACT:\n        if field not in extracted:\n            extracted[field] = None if field != \"Line data.get(field, \"\") for field in main_fields}\n\n    with open(output_path, \"w\", newline='', encoding=\"utf-8\") as csvfile:\n        writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=main_fields)\n        writer.writeheader()\n        writer.writerow(main_row)\n\n        line_items = data.get(\"Line Items\") or []\n        if line_items:\n            csvfile.write(\"\\nLine Items:\\n\")\n Read the file into memory\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as f:\n        file_content = f.read()\n\n    # Determine MIME type\n    ext = os.path.splitext(file_path)[1].lower()\n    if ext == \".pdf\":\n        mime_type = \"application/pdf\"\n    elif ext in [\".jpg\", \".jpeg\"]:\n        mime_type = \"image/jpeg\"\n    elif ext == \".png\":\n        mime_type = \"image/png\"\n    elif ext in [\".tif\", \".tiff\"]:\n        mime_type = \"image/tiff\"\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(f\"Unsupported file type: {ext}\")\n\n    client = get_processor_client()\n    name = f\"projects/{PROJECT_ID}/locations/{LOCATION}/processors/{PROCESSOR_ID}\"\n\n    raw_document = documentai.RawDocument(content=file_content, mime_type=mime_type)\n    request = documentai.ProcessRequest(name=name, raw_document=raw_document)\n    result = client.process_document(request=request)\n    document = result.document\n    return document\n\n# ------------------------------\n# FIELD EXTRACTION\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef extract_fields(document: documentai.Document) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Extracts specified fields from the Document AI response.\n    Handles missing fields gracefully.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def get_text(text_anchor: documentai.Document.TextAnchor) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Helper to get text from a documentai.Document.TextAnchor.\n        \"\"\"\n        response_text = \"\"\n        if not text_anchor.text_segments:\n            return \"\"\n        for segment in text_anchor.text_segments:\n            start_index = segment.start_index\n            end_index = segment.end_index\n            response_text += document.text[start_index:end_index]\n        return response_text.strip()\n\n    # Collect all possible keys in line items\n            all_keys = set()\n            for item in line_items:\n                all_keys.update(item.keys())\n            all_keys = list(all_keys)\n            line_item_writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=all_keys)\n            line_item_writer.writeheader()\n            for item in line_items:\n                line_item_writer.writerow(item)\n\n# ------------------------------\n# MAIN SCRIPT\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"Extract specified fields from supplier invoices using Google Document AI.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"input_file\",\n        help=\"Path to the invoice file (PDF or image) to process.\"\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--output\",\n        help=\"Path to the output file (JSON or CSV).\",\n        required=True\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--format\",\n        choices=[\"json\", \"csv\"],\n        default=\"json\",\n        help=\"Output format: json or csv (default: json).\"\n    )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    #
